## FAQ

<details>
<summary><strong>How often is this list updated?</strong></summary>

Once a day. A GitHub Action pulls new internship postings from Dreamwork's public API, which crawls company career pages directly (Greenhouse, Lever, Ashby, Workday, and others). Use <kbd>Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd>F</kbd> for software engineering, data science, ML, product, or design roles.

</details>

<details>
<summary><strong>Which season are these internships for?</strong></summary>

Whatever companies are hiring for right now. As of mid-2026 that is mostly Fall 2026, Spring 2027, and early Summer 2027 openings. New season postings appear here the day the crawler first sees them.

</details>

<details>
<summary><strong>Graduating soon?</strong></summary>

The companion list, <a href="https://github.com/dreamworkhq/New-Grad-Software-Engineer-Jobs">New Grad Software Engineer Jobs</a>, covers entry-level full-time roles with the same daily refresh.

</details>

<details>
<summary><strong>Can a tool apply to these for me?</strong></summary>

Yes. <a href="https://www.dreamworkhq.com/?utm_source=github&utm_medium=faq&utm_campaign=gh-tech-internships-2026">Dreamwork</a> matches your resume against every listing here, tailors each application, and can submit them for you. Seeing your matches is free.

</details>

## How this list is built

A [GitHub Action](.github/workflows/update.yml) runs once a day. It queries Dreamwork's public listings API, filters for tech internships (software engineering, data science, security, product, design) in the United States, removes duplicates, and rewrites this README. The raw snapshot lives in [`data/listings.json`](data/listings.json). Listings are crawled directly from company career pages and ATS boards (Greenhouse, Lever, Ashby, Workday, and others), so links go to real, currently open postings. Found a bad listing? [Open an issue](../../issues).
